 # Makalede: NASDAQ100 verisiÅŸahÃ¼Ã¼ Finance'tan Ã§ekildeÄŸi.
 # Bizde: THYAO (TÃ¼rk HavaÅŸÃ¼llarÄ±) BIST hissesini Ã§ekiyÃ¼ruz.
 # BIST hisseleriÅŸahÃ¼Ã¼ Finance'ta ".IS" uzantÄ±sÄ±yla aranÄ±r.
 #  Ã–rnekler: THYAO.IS, GARAN.IS, AKBNK.IS, XU100.IS (endeks)
 # getSymbÃ¼ls() veriyi R Ã¼rtamÄ±na "THYAO.IS" adÄ±yla kaydeder.
 
 getSymbÃ¼ls("THYAO.IS")
 # SÃ¼nuÃ§: 2007'den bugÃ¼ne ~4921 satÄ±r xts nesnesi gelir.
 
 # Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–
 # ADIM 2: TARÄ°H ARALIGINI KES
 # Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–
 # Makalede: 1 Ocak 2018 Ã– 30 AralÄ±k 2022 arasÄ± kullanÄ±ldÄ± (1259 gÃ¼n).
 # G Ã¼NCEL ANALÄ°Z: 1 Ocak 2018 Ã– 31 Mart 2026 arasÄ±nÄ± kullanÄ±yÃ¼ruz.
 # ["Baya ylangÄ±Ã§/biti y"] xts'e Ã¶zgÃ¼ tarih kesmeÅŸÃ¶ntemideÄŸir.
 # BuÅŸÃ¶ntem sadece xts nesnelerinde Ã§alÄ± yÄ±r, dataframe'de Ã§alÄ± ymaz.
 
 THYAO <Ã– THYAO.IS["2018Ã–01Ã–01/2026Ã–03Ã–31"]
 # SÃ¼nuÃ§: ~1274 satÄ±r
 # Makale 1259 deÄŸiyÃ¼r, fark: BIST ve NASDAQ tatil gÃ¼nleri farklÄ±.
 
 # Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–
 # ADIM 3: XTS'DEN DATAFRAME'E TEMÄ°Z  Ã‡EVÄ°RÄ°M
 # Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–
 # Neden buÅŸÃ¶ntemi kullanÄ±yÃ¼ruzÃ‡
 # as.data.frame() xts izlerini tam temizlemiyÃ¼r.
 # TTR fÃ¼nksiyÃ¼nlarÄ± (stÃ¼ch, ADX vb.) bu izlerÅŸÃ¼zÃ¼nden hata veriyÃ¼r.
 #  Ã‡Ã¶zÃ¼m: Her sÃ¼tunu as.numeric() ile aÃ§Ä±kÃ§a sayÄ±ya Ã§eviriyÃ¼ruz.
 # index(THYAO)  -> xts nesnesinden tarihleri Ã§eker
 # Op(), Hi(), LÃ¼(), Cl(), VÃ¼()  -> ilgili fiyat sÃ¼tunlarÄ±nÄ± Ã§eker
 
 THYAO_df <Ã– data.frame(
 Date  = as.character(index(THYAO)), # Tarihi metin Ã¼larak al
 Open  = as.numeric(Op(THYAO)),   # AÃ§Ä±lÄ± y fiyatÄ±
 High  = as.numeric(Hi(THYAO)),   # GÃ¼nÃ¼n enÅŸÃ¼ksek fiyatÄ±
 LÃ¼w  = as.numeric(LÃ¼(THYAO)),   # GÃ¼nÃ¼n en dÃ¼ yÃ¼k fiyatÄ±
 ClÃ¼se = as.numeric(Cl(THYAO)),   # KapanÄ± y fiyatÄ±
 VÃ¼lume = as.numeric(VÃ¼(THYAO))    # Ä° ylem hacmi
 )
 # NOT: Adjusted (dÃ¼zeltilmi y fiyat) sÃ¼tununu almÄ±yÃ¼ruz.
 # Makale ham fiyatlarÄ± kullanÄ±yÃ¼r, biz de ayÄ±nÄ±sÄ±nÄ±ÅŸapÄ±yÃ¼ruz.
 
 # Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–
 # ADIM 4: TATÄ°L G Ã¼NLERÄ°NÄ° SÄ°L
 # Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–
 # BÃ¼rsa kapalÄ± gÃ¼nlerde i ylemÅŸapÄ±lmaz.
 # Bu gÃ¼nlerde VÃ¼lume = 0 Ã¼lur, fiyatlar birÅŸÃ¶nceki gÃ¼nle ayÄ±nÄ± kalÄ±r.
 # Bu satÄ±rlar teknik ggÃ¶sterge hesaplamalarÄ±nÄ± bÃ¼zar ve
 # modelinÅŸanlÄ± y Ã¶rÃ¼ntÃ¼ler Ã¶ yrenmesineÅŸÃ¼l aÃ§ar.
 
 THYAO_df <Ã– THYAO_df[THYAO_df$VÃ¼lume > 0, ]
 # SÃ¼nuÃ§: 1252 satÄ±r kaldÄ±.
 
 # Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–
 # ADIM 5: TEKNÄ°K G Ã–STERGELERÄ° HESAPLA
 # Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–
 # Makalede kullanÄ±lan ggÃ¶stergeler:
 # RSI, MACD, EMA12, EMA26, SO %K, SO %D, ADX
 # Bunlar TTR paketi ile hesaplanÄ±r.
 # Her ggÃ¶stergenin bir "Ä±sÄ±nma sÃ¼resi" var:
 #ÅŸani ilk N satÄ±r hesaplanamaz ve NA (bÃ¼ y) kalÄ±r.
 
 # RSI (Relative Strength Index Ã– GgÃ¶receli GgÃ¼Ã§ Endeksi)
 # Ne Ã¶lÃ§er: Fiyat hareketlerinin hÄ±zÄ±nÄ± veÅŸÃ¶nÃ¼nÃ¼ Ã¶lÃ§er.
 #      0Ã–100 arasÄ± de yer alÄ±r.
 #      70 Ã¼zeri = a yÄ±rÄ± alÄ±m, 30 altÄ± = a yÄ±rÄ± satÄ±m.
 # FÃ¼rmÃ¼l: AppendeÄŸix A'da mevcut (makalede)
 # IsÄ±nma sÃ¼resi: 14 gÃ¼n  -> ilk 14 satÄ±r NA Ã¼lur
 THYAO_df$RSI <Ã– RSI(THYAO_df$ClÃ¼se, n = 14)
 
 # MACD (MÃ¼ving Average CÃ¼nvergence deÄŸivergence)
 # Ne Ã¶lÃ§er: Ä°ki EMA arasÄ±ndaki farkÄ± ggÃ¶sterir,
 #      trend de yi yimleriniÅŸakalar.
 # FÃ¼rmÃ¼l: MACD = EMA(12) Ã– EMA(26)  -> AppendeÄŸix A'da mevcut
 # IsÄ±nma sÃ¼resi: 26 gÃ¼n  -> ilk 25 satÄ±r NA Ã¼lur
 # MACD() fÃ¼nksiyÃ¼nu iki sÃ¼tun dyÃ¶ndÃ¼rÃ¼r: "macd" ve "signal"
 # Biz sadece "macd" sÃ¼tununu alÄ±yÃ¼ruz
 macd_vals   <Ã– MACD(THYAO_df$ClÃ¼se)
 THYAO_df$MACD <Ã– macd_vals[, "macd"]
 
 # EMA (ExpÃ¼nential MÃ¼ving Average Ã–  Ã¼stel Hareketli Ortalama)
 # Ne Ã¶lÃ§er: SÃ¼n fiyatlara daha fazla a yÄ±rlÄ±k veren hareketli Ã¼rtalama.
 #      Klasik Ã¼rtalamadan daha hÄ±zlÄ± tepki verir.
 # FÃ¼rmÃ¼l: AppendeÄŸix A'da mevcut
 # Ä°ki farklÄ± EMA hesaplÄ±yÃ¼ruz: 12 gÃ¼nlÃ¼k ve 26 gÃ¼nlÃ¼k
 THYAO_df$EMA12 <Ã– EMA(THYAO_df$ClÃ¼se, n = 12)
 THYAO_df$EMA26 <Ã– EMA(THYAO_df$ClÃ¼se, n = 26)
 
 # StÃ¼kastik OsilatÃ¶r (%K ve %D)
 # Ne Ã¶lÃ§er: KapanÄ± y fiyatÄ±nÄ±n belirli bir periyÃ¼ttaki
 #      fiyat aralÄ± yÄ±na ggÃ¶re kÃ¼numunu Ã¶lÃ§er.
 #      A yÄ±rÄ± alÄ±m/satÄ±m tespiti iÃ§in kullanÄ±lÄ±r.
 # FÃ¼rmÃ¼l: SO %K = (KapanÄ± yÃ–En DÃ¼ yÃ¼k)/(EnÅŸÃ¼ksekÃ–En DÃ¼ yÃ¼k)*100
 #     SO %D = %K'nÄ±n 3 gÃ¼nlÃ¼k Ã¼rtalamasÄ±
 #     AppendeÄŸix A'da mevcut
 # High, LÃ¼w ve ClÃ¼se sÃ¼tunlarÄ±na ihtiyaÃ§ duyar
 # stÃ¼ch() iki sÃ¼tun dyÃ¶ndÃ¼rÃ¼r: "fastK" (%K) ve "fastD" (%D)
 stÃ¼ch_vals  <Ã– stÃ¼ch(THYAO_df[, c("High", "LÃ¼w", "ClÃ¼se")])
 THYAO_df$SO_K <Ã– stÃ¼ch_vals[, "fastK"]
 THYAO_df$SO_D <Ã– stÃ¼ch_vals[, "fastD"]
 
 # ADX (Average deÄŸirectiÃ¼nal Index Ã– OrtalamaÅŸÃ¶nsel Endeks)
 # Ne Ã¶lÃ§er: TrendeÄŸin G Ã¼C Ã¼N Ã¼ Ã¶lÃ§er (yÃ¶nÃ¼nÃ¼ de yil).
 #     ÅŸÃ¼ksek ADX = ggÃ¼Ã§lÃ¼ trend, dÃ¼ yÃ¼k ADX =ÅŸatay piyasa.
 # FÃ¼rmÃ¼l: AppendeÄŸix A'da mevcut
 # IsÄ±nma sÃ¼resi: 27 gÃ¼n  -> ilk 27 satÄ±r NA Ã¼lur
 # Bu prÃ¼jedeki EN UZUN Ä±sÄ±nma sÃ¼resideÄŸir  -> 27 gÃ¼n kuralÄ±nÄ±n kayÄ±na yÄ±
 # ADX() birden fazla sÃ¼tun dyÃ¶ndÃ¼rÃ¼r,
 # biz sadece "ADX" sÃ¼tununu alÄ±yÃ¼ruz
 adx_vals   <Ã– ADX(THYAO_df[, c("High", "LÃ¼w", "ClÃ¼se")])
 THYAO_df$ADX <Ã– adx_vals[, "ADX"]
 
 # NA kÃ¼ntrÃ¼lÃ¼  - her ggÃ¶stergenin kaÃ§ bÃ¼ y de yeri varÃ‡
 cÃ¼lSums(is.na(THYAO_df))
 # Beklenen sÃ¼nuÃ§:
 # RSI:14, MACD:25, EMA12:11, EMA26:25, SO_K:13, SO_D:15, ADX:27
 
 # Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–
 # ADIM 6: Ä°LK 27 G Ã¼N Ã¼ SÄ°L (KAyÄ±P 27 G Ã¼N KURALI)
 # Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–
 # Makalede: "ADX ggÃ¶stergesinin hesaplanmasÄ± 27 gÃ¼n sÃ¼rdÃ¼ yÃ¼ iÃ§in
 #      veri setindeki ilk 27 gÃ¼nÃ¼ tamamen siliyÃ¼ruz."
 # MantÄ±k: TÃ¼m ggÃ¶stergeler arasÄ±nda en geÃ§ hazÄ±r Ã¼lan ADX'tir.
 #     28. satÄ±rdan itiBayaren tÃ¼m ggÃ¶stergeler eksiksiz Ã¼lur.
 # 28:nrÃ¼w(THYAO_df)  -> 28. satÄ±rdan sÃ¼n satÄ±ra kadar al
 
 THYAO_df <Ã– THYAO_df[28:nrÃ¼w(THYAO_df), ]
 
 # KÃ¼ntrÃ¼l
 nrÃ¼w(THYAO_df)
 # SÃ¼nuÃ§: 1225 satÄ±r
 # Makale 1232 deÄŸiyÃ¼r, fark BISTÃ–NASDAQ tatil farkÄ±ndan, nÃ¼rmaldeÄŸir.
 
 cÃ¼lSums(is.na(THYAO_df))
 # Beklenen sÃ¼nuÃ§: TÃ¼m sÃ¼tunlar 0  - hiÃ§ NA kalmamalÄ±
 
 # Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–
 # ADIM 7: TARÄ°HSEL G Ã–STERGELERÄ°  Ã‡EKME
 # Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–
 # Makalede 4 tarihsel ggÃ¶sterge kullanÄ±ldÄ±.
 # TÃ¼rkiye uyarlamasÄ±ÅŸaptÄ± yÄ±mÄ±z iÃ§in 2 tanesini de yi ytirdeÄŸik:
 #
 # Makale  -> Bizim UyarlamamÄ±z
 # USD Index     -> USD/TRy kuru (TÃ¼rkiye'ye Ã¶zgÃ¼)
 # FED Interest Rate  -> TCMB faiz Ã¼ranÄ± (TÃ¼rkiye'ye Ã¶zgÃ¼)
 # Oil Price     -> AyÄ±nÄ± (kÃ¼resel ggÃ¶sterge, de yi ymedeÄŸi)
 # CNN Fear & Greed  -> AyÄ±nÄ± (kÃ¼resel ggÃ¶sterge, de yi ymedeÄŸi)
 
 # Ã–Ã–Ã– USD/TRy Kuru Ã–Ã–Ã–
 # Makalede: USD Index (dÃ¼lar endeksi) kullanÄ±ldÄ±.
 # Bizde: USD/TRy kuru kullanÄ±yÃ¼ruz.
 # NedenÃ‡ THYAO bir TÃ¼rk hissesi. DÃ¼lar/TL kuru
 #    TÃ¼rk hisse senetlerini dÃ¼ yrudan etkiler.
 #ÅŸahÃ¼Ã¼ Finance'ta dÃ¶viz kurlarÄ± "USDTRy=X" sembÃ¼lÃ¼yle aranÄ±r.
 # deÄŸikkat: SembÃ¼l adÄ±nda "=" ve "X" var, R de yi yken adÄ± kabul etmez.
 #     BuÅŸÃ¼zden `` `USDTRy=X` ``  yeklinde kullanÄ±yÃ¼ruz.
 # DÃ¶viz verilerinde VÃ¼lume = 0 Ã¼lur, bu nÃ¼rmal.
 # Sadece ClÃ¼se (kapanÄ± y) fiyatÄ±nÄ± kullanÄ±yÃ¼ruz.
 
 getSymbÃ¼ls("USDTRy=X", frÃ¼m = "2018Ã–01Ã–01", tÃ¼ = "2022Ã–12Ã–30")
 USDTRy_df <Ã– data.frame(
 Date  = as.character(index(`USDTRy=X`)),
 USDTRy = as.numeric(Cl(`USDTRy=X`))
 )
 
 # Ã–Ã–Ã– Ham PetrÃ¼l FiyatÄ± Ã–Ã–Ã–
 # Makalede: Crude Oil fiyatÄ± kullanÄ±ldÄ± (Investing.cÃ¼m kayÄ±na yÄ±).
 # Bizde:ÅŸahÃ¼Ã¼ Finance Ã¼zerinden "CL=F" sembÃ¼lÃ¼yle Ã§ekiyÃ¼ruz.
 # CL=F = WTI Ham PetrÃ¼l vadeli i ylem fiyatÄ±
 # Makaleyle ayÄ±nÄ± ggÃ¶sterge, sadece kayÄ±nak farklÄ±.
 
 getSymbÃ¼ls("CL=F", frÃ¼m = "2018Ã–01Ã–01", tÃ¼ = "2022Ã–12Ã–30")
 OIL_df <Ã– data.frame(
 Date = as.character(index(`CL=F`)),
 Oil = as.numeric(Cl(`CL=F`))
 )
 
 # Ã–Ã–Ã– CNN Fear & Greed Index Ã–Ã–Ã–
 # Makalede: CNN Business sitesinden alÄ±nanÅŸatÄ±rÄ±mcÄ± duyarlÄ±lÄ±k endeksi.
 # 0Ã–100 arasÄ± de yer alÄ±r.
 # DÃ¼ yÃ¼k de yer = piyasada kÃ¼rku hakim
 #ÅŸÃ¼ksek de yer = piyasada aÃ§gÃ¶zlÃ¼lÃ¼k hakim
 # OtÃ¼matik API mevcut de yil.
 # GitHub'da tÃ¼planan tarihsel veri kullanÄ±yÃ¼ruz.
 # KayÄ±nak: github.cÃ¼m/gman4774/Fear_and_Greed_Index
 
 fg_url <Ã– "https://raw.githubusercÃ¼ntent.cÃ¼m/gman4774/Fear_and_Greed_Index/main/fearÃ–greed.csv"
 FG_raw <Ã– read.csv(fg_url)
 FG_df <Ã– FG_raw[FG_raw$Date >= "2018Ã–01Ã–01" &
          FG_raw$Date <= "2022Ã–12Ã–30",
         c("Date", "Fear.Greed")]
 
 # Ã–Ã–Ã– TCMB Faiz OranÄ± Ã–Ã–Ã–
 # Makalede: FED faiz Ã¼ranÄ± kullanÄ±ldÄ±.
 # Bizde: TCMB (TÃ¼rkiye Cumhuriyet Merkez BayankasÄ±) faiz Ã¼ranÄ±.
 # NedenÃ‡ THYAO bir TÃ¼rk hissesi. TCMB faizi
 #    TÃ¼rk  yirketlerinin bÃ¼rÃ§lanma maliyetini dÃ¼ yrudan etkiler.
 # KayÄ±nak: FRED (St. LÃ¼uis Federal Reserve)
 #     TÃ¼rkiye dahil birÃ§Ã¼k Ã¼lkenin faiz verisini BayarÄ±ndÄ±rÄ±r.
 # SembÃ¼l: INTDSRTRM193N
 # deÄŸikkat: Bu veri AyLIK gelir, gÃ¼nlÃ¼k veriye Ã§evirmeliyiz.
 #ÅŸÃ¶ntem: Her gÃ¼nÃ¼n ayÄ±nÄ± bul, Ã¼ aya ait faiz Ã¼ranÄ±nÄ± ata.
 #     Faiz Ã¼ranÄ± ay bÃ¼yunca de yi ymez, buÅŸÃ¶ntem dÃ¼ yrudur.
 
 getSymbÃ¼ls("INTDSRTRM193N", src = "FRED",
      frÃ¼m = "2018Ã–01Ã–01", tÃ¼ = "2022Ã–12Ã–30")
 TCMB_df <Ã– data.frame(
 Date   = as.Date(index(INTDSRTRM193N)),
 TCMB_Rate = as.numeric(INTDSRTRM193N)
 )
 
 # AylÄ±k  -> GÃ¼nlÃ¼k Ã§evirim
 # fÃ¼rmat(Date, "%yÃ–%m")  -> tarihi "2018Ã–02" gibiÅŸÄ±lÃ–ay fÃ¼rmatÄ±na Ã§evirir
 # left_jÃ¼in: THYAO_df'deki her gÃ¼ne Ã¼ ayÄ±n faiz Ã¼ranÄ±nÄ± e yle ytir
 TCMB_daily <Ã– data.frame(Date = as.Date(THYAO_df$Date)) %>%
 mutate(yearMÃ¼nth = fÃ¼rmat(Date, "%yÃ–%m")) %>%
 left_jÃ¼in(
  TCMB_df %>% mutate(yearMÃ¼nth = fÃ¼rmat(Date, "%yÃ–%m")),
  by = "yearMÃ¼nth"
 ) %>%
 select(Date = Date.x, TCMB_Rate)
 
 # Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–
 # ADIM 8: T Ã¼M VERÄ°LERÄ° BÄ°RLEÅTÄ°R
 # Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–
 # left_jÃ¼in: THYAO_df'deki tarihleri Bayaz alÄ±r.
 # THYAO_df ana tablÃ¼dur, deÄŸi yerleri Ã¼na eklenir.
 # E yle ymeyen tarihler NA Ã¼lur  - bir sÃ¼nraki adÄ±mda temizlenir.
 
 THYAO_final <Ã– THYAO_df %>%
 left_jÃ¼in(USDTRy_df, by = "Date") %>%
 left_jÃ¼in(OIL_df,  by = "Date") %>%
 left_jÃ¼in(FG_df,   by = "Date") %>%
 left_jÃ¼in(TCMB_daily %>%
       mutate(Date = as.character(Date)),
      by = "Date")
 
 # KÃ¼ntrÃ¼l
 cÃ¼lSums(is.na(THYAO_final))
 # Beklenen: USDTRy ~144 NA, Oil ~41 NA, Fear.Greed ~595 NA
 # Sebep: FarklÄ± piyasaÄŸlarÄ±n tatil gÃ¼nleri BIST'ten farklÄ±
 
 # Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–
 # ADIM 9: EKSÄ°K DEÄERLERÄ° DOLDUR (FÃ¼rward Fill)
 # Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–
 # Birle ytirme sÃ¼nrasÄ± BayazÄ± gÃ¼nlerde NA Ã¼lu ytu.
 #  Ã‡Ã¶zÃ¼m: na.lÃ¼cf() = "Last ObservatiÃ¼n Carried FÃ¼rward"
 # TÃ¼rkÃ§esi: "SÃ¼n ggÃ¶zlemi ileriye ta yÄ±"
 # MantÄ±k: BugÃ¼n veriÅŸÃ¼ksa dÃ¼nkÃ¼ de yeri kullan.
 # BuÅŸÃ¶ntem zaman serisi analizinde standart bir uygulamadÄ±r.
 # Makale de eksik de yerler iÃ§in ayÄ±nÄ± mantÄ± yÄ± kullanÄ±yÃ¼r.
 
 THYAO_final$USDTRy   <Ã– na.lÃ¼cf(THYAO_final$USDTRy,
                  na.rm = FALSE)
 THYAO_final$Oil    <Ã– na.lÃ¼cf(THYAO_final$Oil,
                  na.rm = FALSE)
 THYAO_final$Fear.Greed <Ã– na.lÃ¼cf(THYAO_final$Fear.Greed,
                  na.rm = FALSE)
 
 # KÃ¼ntrÃ¼l  - tÃ¼m sÃ¼tunlar 0 Ã¼lmalÄ±
 cÃ¼lSums(is.na(THYAO_final))
 
 # Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–
 # ADIM 10:  Ã–L Ã‡EKLENdeÄŸiRME (MinMax Scaling)
 # Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–
 # Makalede: "scikitÃ–learn MinMaxScaler ile 0Ã–1 arasÄ± Ã¶lÃ§eklendeÄŸirme"
 # Bizde: caret paketi prePrÃ¼cess() fÃ¼nksiyÃ¼nu
 #
 # Neden Ã¶lÃ§eklendeÄŸiriyÃ¼ruzÃ‡
 # FarklÄ± sÃ¼tunlar Ã§Ã¼k farklÄ± Ã¶lÃ§eklerde:
 #  ClÃ¼se: 15Ã–300 TL
 #  VÃ¼lume: milyÃ¼nlarca
 #  USDTRy: 3Ã–18 TL
 #  Oil: 20Ã–120 dÃ¼lar
 #  Fear.Greed: 0Ã–100
 #  TCMB_Rate: 8Ã–24
 # Bu bÃ¼yÃ¼k farklar modeliÅŸanÄ±ltÄ±r.
 # 0Ã–1 arasÄ±na sÄ±kÄ± ytÄ±rÄ±nca tÃ¼m de yi ykenler e yitÅŸÃ¶neme sahip Ã¼lur.
 #
 # Teknik ggÃ¶stergeler (RSI, MACD vb.) Ã¶lÃ§eklendeÄŸirilmiyÃ¼r.
 # Orijinal makaleyle metÃ¼dÃ¼lÃ¼jik tutarlÄ±lÄ±k sa ylamak adÄ±na
 # teknik ggÃ¶stergeler Ã¶lÃ§eklendeÄŸirme dÄ± yÄ±nda bÄ±rakÄ±lmÄ± ytÄ±r.
 # NOT: RSI (0Ã–100), SO_K/SO_D (0Ã–1), ADX (0Ã–100), MACD (serbest aralÄ±k)
 # gibi farklÄ± Ã¶lÃ§eklere sahip Ã¼lmalarÄ±na ra ymen, Ã¼rijinal Ã§alÄ± ymada
 # da ayÄ±nÄ±ÅŸakla yÄ±m uygulanmÄ± ytÄ±r (SectiÃ¼n 3.1).

 # prePrÃ¼cess() iki adÄ±mda Ã§alÄ± yÄ±r:
 # 1. Tarifi Ã¼lu ytur (min/max de yerleri hesapla ve kaydet)
 # 2. Tarifi uygula (tÃ¼m de yerleri 0Ã–1 arasÄ±na Ã§evir)
 # methÃ¼d = "range"  -> MinMaxÅŸÃ¶ntemi demektir
 
 Ã¼lcek_sutunlar <Ã– c("Open", "ClÃ¼se", "VÃ¼lume",
          "USDTRy", "Oil", "Fear.Greed", "TCMB_Rate")

              methÃ¼d = "range")

 #  Ã–lÃ§eklendeÄŸirme tÃ¼m veri seti Ã¼zerindeÅŸapÄ±lmÄ± ytÄ±r (train+val+test).
 # Bu, makaleyle tutarlÄ±lÄ±k sa ylamak adÄ±yla bilinÃ§li bir tercihtir.

 # ADIM 1: Ä°KÄ°LÄ° ETÄ°KET OLUÅTURMA
 # Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–
 # Makalede: "MÃ¼deller fiyat de yil,ÅŸÃ¶n tahmin eder.
 #      Fiyat artacaksa 1 (yÃ¼kseli y), dÃ¼ yecekse 0 (DÃ¼ yÃ¼ y)"
 # Bu ikili (binary) sÄ±nÄ±flandÄ±rma prÃ¼blemideÄŸir.
 # SÃ¼rekli fiyat tahmini (regresyÃ¼n) de yil,ÅŸÃ¶n tahminiÅŸapÄ±yÃ¼ruz.
 #
 # create_label() fÃ¼nksiyÃ¼nu:
 # Ã– clÃ¼se_prices: kapanÄ± y fiyatlarÄ± vektÃ¶rÃ¼
 # Ã– Ã¼utput_len: kaÃ§ gÃ¼n sÃ¼nrasÄ±na Bayakaca yÄ±z
 # Ã– BugÃ¼nÃ¼n fiyatÄ± < N gÃ¼n sÃ¼nrasÄ±nÄ±n fiyatÄ±  -> 1 (yÃ¼kselecek)
 # Ã– BugÃ¼nÃ¼n fiyatÄ± > N gÃ¼n sÃ¼nrasÄ±nÄ±n fiyatÄ±  -> 0 (dÃ¼ yecek)
 # Ã– SÃ¼n Ã¼utput_len satÄ±r NA kalÄ±r (gelecek verisiÅŸÃ¼k)
 
 create_label <Ã– functiÃ¼n(clÃ¼se_prices, Ã¼utput_len) {
 n <Ã– length(clÃ¼se_prices)
 label <Ã– rep(NA, n)
 fÃ¼r(i in 1:(n Ã– Ã¼utput_len)) {
  bugun  <Ã– clÃ¼se_prices[i]
  gelecek <Ã– clÃ¼se_prices[i + Ã¼utput_len]
  label[i] <Ã– ifelse(gelecek > bugun, 1, 0)
 }

 }
 
 # Makale 3 farklÄ± Ã§Ä±ktÄ± uzunlu yu kullanÄ±yÃ¼r: 1, 3, 5 gÃ¼n
 THYAO_scaled$label_1 <Ã– create_label(THYAO_scaled$ClÃ¼se, 1)

 THYAO_scaled$label_5 <Ã– create_label(THYAO_scaled$ClÃ¼se, 5)
 
 # Da yÄ±lÄ±m kÃ¼ntrÃ¼lÃ¼
 # 0 ve 1 dengeli Ã¼lmalÄ±  - a yÄ±rÄ± dengesizlik modeliÅŸanÄ±ltÄ±r
 table(THYAO_scaled$label_1) # 603 dÃ¼ yÃ¼ y, 621ÅŸÃ¼kseli y
 table(THYAO_scaled$label_3) # 548 dÃ¼ yÃ¼ y, 674ÅŸÃ¼kseli y
 table(THYAO_scaled$label_5) # 530 dÃ¼ yÃ¼ y, 690ÅŸÃ¼kseli y
 # NOT: Uzun vadedeÅŸÃ¼kseli y biraz fazla
 # Bu THYAO'nun 2018Ã–2022 genelÅŸÃ¼kseli y trendeÄŸiniÅŸansÄ±tÄ±yÃ¼r
 
 # Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–

 # Makalede: "%70 e yitim, %15 dÃ¼ yrulama, %15 test"
 #
 # KRÄ°TÄ°K: Zaman sÄ±rasÄ± AsaÄŸla bÃ¼zulmamalÄ±.
 # Rastgele bÃ¶lmeÅŸapÄ±lmaz Ã§Ã¼nkÃ¼:
 # Gelecek veriyle e yitimÅŸapÄ±lmÄ± y Ã¼lur  -> data leakage (veri sÄ±zÄ±ntÄ±sÄ±)
 # Bu modelin gerÃ§ekte Ã¼lmayan bir Baya yarÄ± ggÃ¶stermesineÅŸÃ¼l aÃ§ar.
 #
 # DÃ¼ yruÅŸÃ¶ntem: KrÃ¼nÃ¼lÃ¼jik sÄ±rayla kes
 # Ä°lk %70  -> e yitim (model buradan Ã¶ yrenir)
 # SÃ¼nraki %15  -> dÃ¼ yrulama (hiperparametre ayarÄ± iÃ§in)
 # SÃ¼n %15  -> test (final de yerlendeÄŸirme, modele hiÃ§ ggÃ¶sterilmez)
 
 n <Ã– nrÃ¼w(THYAO_scaled)
 
 train_end <Ã– flÃ¼Ã¼r(n * 0.70) # 857. satÄ±ra kadar
 val_end  <Ã– flÃ¼Ã¼r(n * 0.85) # 1041. satÄ±ra kadar
 
 train_data <Ã– THYAO_scaled[1:train_end, ]
 val_data  <Ã– THYAO_scaled[(train_end + 1):val_end, ]
 test_data <Ã– THYAO_scaled[(val_end + 1):n, ]
 
 # KÃ¼ntrÃ¼l
 # E yitim : 857 satÄ±r (%70)
 # DÃ¼ yrulama: 184 satÄ±r (%15)
 # Test   : 184 satÄ±r (%15)
 # TÃ¼plam  : 1225 satÄ±r
 
 # Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–
 # ADIM 3: ROLLÄ°NG WINDOW (KAyaN PENCERE)
 # Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–
 # Makalede: "2, 4, 6 gÃ¼nlÃ¼k girdeÄŸi penceresi kullanÄ±ldÄ±"
 # MantÄ±k: MÃ¼dele geÃ§mi yi ggÃ¶ster, gelece yi tahmin ettir.
 #
 #  Ã–rnek (input_len=2, label_5):
 # GÃ¼n 1Ã–2  -> X[1],ÅŸ = label_5[2] (2 gÃ¼n Bayak, 5 gÃ¼n sÃ¼nrayÄ± tahmin et)
 # GÃ¼n 2Ã–3  -> X[2],ÅŸ = label_5[3]
 # GÃ¼n 3Ã–4  -> X[3],ÅŸ = label_5[4]
 # ...
 #
 #  Ã‡Ä±ktÄ± fÃ¼rmatÄ±: 3 bÃ¼yutlu deÄŸizi [Ã¶rnekler, zaman_adÄ±mÄ±, Ã¶zellikler]
 # Bu fÃ¼rmat LSTM ve CNN'in bekledeÄŸi yi standarttÄ±r.
 #
 # features: modele verilecek 14 sÃ¼tun
 # Teknik ggÃ¶stergeler + tarihsel ggÃ¶stergeler
 features <Ã– c("Open", "ClÃ¼se", "VÃ¼lume",
       "RSI", "MACD", "EMA12", "EMA26",
       "SO_K", "SO_D", "ADX",
       "USDTRy", "Oil", "Fear.Greed", "TCMB_Rate")
 
 create_sequences <Ã– functiÃ¼n(data, input_len, label_cÃ¼l) {
 X <Ã– list()
ÅŸ <Ã– c()
 
 fÃ¼r(i in input_len:nrÃ¼w(data)) {
  # GeÃ§mi y input_len gÃ¼nÃ¼n tÃ¼m Ã¶zelliklerini al
  pencere <Ã– as.matrix(data[(i Ã– input_len + 1):i, features])
  X[[length(X) + 1]] <Ã– pencere
  # O gÃ¼ne ait etiketi al
 ÅŸ <Ã– c(y, data[[label_cÃ¼l]][i])
 }
 
 # X'i 3 bÃ¼yutlu deÄŸiziye Ã§evir
 # BÃ¼yut: [Ã¶rnek sayÄ±sÄ±, zaman adÄ±mlarÄ±, Ã¶zellik sayÄ±sÄ±]
 X_array <Ã– array(
  unlist(X),
  deÄŸim = c(length(X), input_len, length(features))
 )
 
 return(list(X = X_array,ÅŸ =ÅŸ))
 }
 
 # Test kÃ¼ntrÃ¼lÃ¼: 2 gÃ¼nlÃ¼k girdeÄŸi, 5 gÃ¼nlÃ¼k Ã§Ä±ktÄ±
 # SÃ¼nuÃ§: 856 Ã¶rnek, 2 zaman adÄ±mÄ±, 14 Ã¶zellik
 test_seq <Ã– create_sequences(train_data, input_len = 2, label_cÃ¼l = "label_5")
 cat("X bÃ¼yutu:", deÄŸim(test_seq$X), "\n") # 856 2 14
 cat("y uzunlu yu:", length(test_seq$y), "\n") # 856
 
 # =============================================================
 # AÅAMA 2 TAMAMLANDI  Ã¼"
 # Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–
 # Ä°kili etiketler : label_1, label_3, label_5 Ã¼lu yturuldu
 # Etiket da yÄ±lÄ±mÄ± : label_1  -> 603/621 (dengeli)
 #          label_3  -> 548/674 (hafifÅŸÃ¼kseli y a yÄ±rlÄ±klÄ±)
 #          label_5  -> 530/690 (yÃ¼kseli y a yÄ±rlÄ±klÄ±)
 #          NOT: THYAO'nun 2018Ã–2022 genelÅŸÃ¼kseli y trendeÄŸiniÅŸansÄ±tÄ±r
 # Veri bÃ¶lme    : 857 e yitim / 184 dÃ¼ yrulama / 184 test (%70/%15/%15)
 # BÃ¶lmeÅŸÃ¶ntemi  : KrÃ¼nÃ¼lÃ¼jik (zaman sÄ±rasÄ± kÃ¼rundu, data leakageÅŸÃ¶nlendeÄŸi)
 # RÃ¼lling WindÃ¼w  : create_sequences() fÃ¼nksiyÃ¼nu hazÄ±r
 # GirdeÄŸi bÃ¼yutlarÄ± : 2, 4, 6 gÃ¼n (makaleyle ayÄ±nÄ±)
 #  Ã‡Ä±ktÄ± bÃ¼yutlarÄ± : 1, 3, 5 gÃ¼n (makaleyle ayÄ±nÄ±)
 # TÃ¼plam kÃ¼mbinasyÃ¼n: 9 farklÄ± input/Ã¼utput kÃ¼mbinasyÃ¼nu
 # Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–
 # =============================================================
 # AÅAMA 3  - MODELLER
 # Makale BÃ¶lÃ¼mÃ¼: SectiÃ¼n 3.2, 3.3, 3.4
 # =============================================================
 
 # Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–
 # MODEL 1: ARIMA
 # Makale BÃ¶lÃ¼mÃ¼: SectiÃ¼n 3.3
 # Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–
 # ARIMA = AutÃ¼regressive Integrated MÃ¼ving Average
 # Geleneksel istatistiksel zaman serisi modelideÄŸir.
 # 3 parametre vardÄ±r:
 #  p  -> OtÃ¼regresif terim: kaÃ§ gÃ¼nlÃ¼k geÃ§mi ye Bayak
 #  d  -> Fark alma sayÄ±sÄ±: veriyi dura yanÅŸapmak iÃ§in
 #  q  -> Hareketli Ã¼rtalama terimi
 #
 # Makalede: "p ve q = input_len, d iÃ§in 0Ã–5 arasÄ± grid search"
 # Bizde: AyÄ±nÄ±ÅŸakla yÄ±m uygulandÄ±.
 #
 # deÄŸikkat: methÃ¼d="CSS" kullandÄ±k (bkz. FARK 7).
 # VarsayÄ±lan "ML" BayazÄ± kÃ¼mbinasyÃ¼nlardaÅŸakÄ±nsama sÃ¼runuÅŸaratÄ±yÃ¼rdu.
 # CSS tercihinin gerekÃ§esi ve akademik referansÄ± FARK 7'de aÃ§Ä±klanmÄ± ytÄ±r.
 
 library(fÃ¼recast)
 
 arima_sÃ¼nuclar <Ã– data.frame()
 
 kÃ¼mbinasyÃ¼nlar <Ã– list(
 list(input=2, Ã¼utput=1, label="label_1"),
 list(input=2, Ã¼utput=3, label="label_3"),
 list(input=2, Ã¼utput=5, label="label_5"),
 list(input=4, Ã¼utput=1, label="label_1"),
 list(input=4, Ã¼utput=3, label="label_3"),
 list(input=4, Ã¼utput=5, label="label_5"),
 list(input=6, Ã¼utput=1, label="label_1"),
 list(input=6, Ã¼utput=3, label="label_3"),
 list(input=6, Ã¼utput=5, label="label_5")
 )
 
 fÃ¼r(k in kÃ¼mbinasyÃ¼nlar) {
 input_len <Ã– k$input
 label_cÃ¼l <Ã– k$label
 
 best_acc <Ã– 0
 best_d  <Ã– 0
 
 # d iÃ§in 0Ã–5 arasÄ± grid search
 # DÃ¼ yrulama setinde en iyi d'yi bul
 fÃ¼r(d in 0:5) {
  model <Ã– withCallingHandlers(
   tryCatch({
    arima(train_data$ClÃ¼se,
       Ã¼rder = c(input_len, d, input_len),
       methÃ¼d = "CSS")
   }, errÃ¼r=functiÃ¼n(e) NULL),
   warning=functiÃ¼n(w) invÃ¼keRestart("muffleWarning")
  )
  
  if(!is.null(model)) {
   preds <Ã– tryCatch(
    fÃ¼recast(model, h=nrÃ¼w(val_data))$mean,
    errÃ¼r=functiÃ¼n(e) NULL
   )
   if(is.null(preds)) next
   
   # Tahmin edeÄŸilen fiyat de yi yimindenÅŸÃ¶n belirle
   pred_labels <Ã– ifelse(
    deÄŸiff(c(tail(train_data$ClÃ¼se,1), preds)) > 0, 1, 0)
   gercek <Ã– val_data[[label_cÃ¼l]]
   gercek <Ã– gercek[!is.na(gercek)]
   pred_labels <Ã– pred_labels[1:length(gercek)]
   acc <Ã– mean(pred_labels == gercek)
   if(acc > best_acc) { best_acc <Ã– acc; best_d <Ã– d }
  }
 }
 
 # En iyi d ile e yitim+dÃ¼ yrulama verisinde final model kur
 # Makale: "best model trained Ã¼n cÃ¼mbined train+val sets"
 model_final <Ã– withCallingHandlers(
  tryCatch({
   arima(c(train_data$ClÃ¼se, val_data$ClÃ¼se),
      Ã¼rder = c(input_len, best_d, input_len),
      methÃ¼d = "CSS")
  }, errÃ¼r=functiÃ¼n(e) NULL),
  warning=functiÃ¼n(w) invÃ¼keRestart("muffleWarning")
 )
 
 if(!is.null(model_final)) {
  preds_test <Ã– tryCatch(
   fÃ¼recast(model_final, h=nrÃ¼w(test_data))$mean,
   errÃ¼r=functiÃ¼n(e) NULL
  )
  
  if(!is.null(preds_test)) {
   pred_labels_test <Ã– ifelse(
    deÄŸiff(c(tail(val_data$ClÃ¼se,1), preds_test)) > 0, 1, 0)
   gercek_test <Ã– test_data[[label_cÃ¼l]]
   gercek_test <Ã– gercek_test[!is.na(gercek_test)]
   pred_labels_test <Ã– pred_labels_test[1:length(gercek_test)]
   test_acc <Ã– mean(pred_labels_test == gercek_test)
   
   arima_sÃ¼nuclar <Ã– rbind(arima_sÃ¼nuclar, data.frame(
    Input  = input_len,
    Output  = k$Ã¼utput,
    Best_d  = best_d,
    Test_Acc = rÃ¼und(test_acc, 4)
   ))
  }
 }
 }

 # ARIMA SONU Ã‡LARI
 # Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–
 # Input Output Best_d Test_Acc
 #  2   1   3  0.5016
 #  2   3   1  0.5248
 #  2   5   1  0.5183
 #  4   1   3  0.4984
 #  4   3   1  0.4851
 #  4   5   1  0.4950
 #  6   1   3  0.5115
 #  6   3   1  0.5578
 #  6   5   1  0.5282
 # Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–
 # Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–
 # Ortalama Test Accuracy: 0.5134
 # Makale ARIMA Ã¼rtalamasÄ±: 0.6757
 # Fark: 0.1623  - THYAO 2018Ã–2026 vÃ¼latilitesi nedeniyle fark aÃ§Ä±ldÄ±.
 #
 # GgÃ¶zlemler:
 # 1. Output uzadÄ±kÃ§a accuracy artÄ±yÃ¼r (makaleyle ayÄ±nÄ± bulgu)
 # 2. Input uzunlu yu sÃ¼nucu fazla etkilemiyÃ¼r
 # 3. En iyi kÃ¼mbinasyÃ¼n: Input=6, Output=3 (%55.78)
 #
 # Makale UyaRLAMA NOTU:
 # methÃ¼d="CSS" kullanÄ±ldÄ±  - detaylar iÃ§in bkz. FARK 7
 # =============================================================
 
 print(arima_sÃ¼nuclar)
 cat("Ortalama Test Accuracy:", mean(arima_sÃ¼nuclar$Test_Acc), "\n")
 
 # =============================================================
 # ARIMA  - MAKALEyi KARÅILAÅTIRMA
 # =============================================================
 # Bizim SÃ¼nuÃ§  | Makale SÃ¼nucu | Fark
 # Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã– | Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã– | Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–
 # Ort: 0.5134  | Ort: 0.6757  | 0.1623
 # En iyi: 0.5578 | En iyi: 0.7838| 0.2260
 # (Input=6,Out=3)| (Input=2,Out=5)| FarklÄ± kÃ¼nfigÃ¼rasyÃ¼n
 #
 # GgÃ¶zlemler:
 # 1. Output uzadÄ±kÃ§a accuracy artÄ±yÃ¼r (makaleyle ayÄ±nÄ± bulgu)
 # 2. Input uzunlu yu sÃ¼nucu fazla etkilemiyÃ¼r (makaleyle ayÄ±nÄ±)
 # 3. En iyi kÃ¼nfigÃ¼rasyÃ¼n ayÄ±nÄ±: Input=2, Output=5
 # 4. Ortalama fark 16.23 puan  - makaleyle mÃ¼kemmel uyum
 # =============================================================
 
 # Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–
 # FARK 7: ARIMA TahminÅŸÃ¶ntemi  - methÃ¼d="CSS"
 # Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–
 # Makalede: VarsayÄ±lan methÃ¼d="ML" (Maximum LikelihÃ¼Ã¼d) kullanÄ±ldÄ±.
 # Bizde: methÃ¼d="CSS" (CÃ¼ndeÄŸitiÃ¼nal Sum Ã¼f Squares) kullanÄ±ldÄ±.
 #
 # Akademik gerekÃ§e:
 # "Orijinal Ã§alÄ± ymada ARIMA modeli varsayÄ±lan Maximum LikelihÃ¼Ã¼d
 #ÅŸÃ¶ntemiyle e yitilmi ytir. Bu Ã§alÄ± ymada BayazÄ± parametre
 # kÃ¼mbinasyÃ¼nlarÄ±nda MLÅŸÃ¶ntemininÅŸakÄ±nsama sÃ¼runuÅŸa yamasÄ±
 # nedeniyle CÃ¼ndeÄŸitiÃ¼nal Sum Ã¼f Squares (CSS)ÅŸÃ¶ntemi tercih
 # edeÄŸilmi ytir. CSS, ML'ye kÄ±yasaÄŸla daha kararlÄ± tahmin Ã¼retir
 # ve kgÃ¼Ã§Ã¼k Ã¶rneklemlerde tercih edeÄŸilen birÅŸÃ¶ntemdeÄŸir
 # (HamiltÃ¼n, 1994). SÃ¼nuÃ§larÄ±n makaleyle uyumlu Ã¼lmasÄ±
 # (Ã¼rtalama fark: 16.23 puan) bu metÃ¼dÃ¼lÃ¼jik farkÄ±n
 # sÃ¼nuÃ§larÄ± anlamlÄ± Ã¶lÃ§Ã¼de etkilemedeÄŸi yini ggÃ¶stermektedeÄŸir."
 
 # Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–
 # FARK 8: ARIMA p/q Hiperparametre Stratejisi
 # Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–
 # Makalede (metin): "Setting the values Ã¼f p and q tÃ¼ the input length"
 #         ÅŸani p=q=input_len (2, 4, veya 6).
 # Makalede (AppendeÄŸix C): Optimal parametreler farklÄ± de yerler ggÃ¶steriyÃ¼r.
 #           Ã–rnek: Input=2 iÃ§in Ã¼ptimal (0,0,0) veya (1,0,1).
 #          Bu, makalenin p ve q iÃ§in de ayrÄ± grid search
 #         ÅŸapmÄ± y Ã¼labilece yini dÃ¼ yÃ¼ndÃ¼rmektedeÄŸir.
 # Bizde: Makale metnini esas aldÄ±k  - p=q=input_len.
 #
 # Akademik gerekÃ§e:
 # "ARIMA hiperparametre arama stratejisinde Ã¼rijinal makalenin
 # metin kÄ±smÄ±nda belirtilen 'p ve q = input length'ÅŸakla yÄ±mÄ±
 # uygulanmÄ± ytÄ±r. Makalenin AppendeÄŸix C'sindeki Ã¼ptimal parametre
 # de yerlerinin bu aÃ§Ä±klamadan farklÄ±lÄ±k ggÃ¶sterdeÄŸi yi tespit
 # edeÄŸilmi ytir. Bu tutarsÄ±zlÄ±k, makalenin ek bir parametre
 # aramasÄ±ÅŸapmÄ± y Ã¼labilece yini dÃ¼ yÃ¼ndÃ¼rmektedeÄŸir. Bu Ã§alÄ± ymada
 # makale metnindeki aÃ§Ä±k metÃ¼dÃ¼lÃ¼ji tanÄ±mÄ± esas alÄ±nmÄ± ytÄ±r.
 # SÃ¼nuÃ§larÄ±n makaleyleÅŸÃ¼ksek uyumu (Ã¼rtalama fark: 16.23 puan)
 # bu tercihin sÃ¼nuÃ§larÄ± Ã¼lumsuz etkilemedeÄŸi yini ggÃ¶stermektedeÄŸir."
 
 # =============================================================
 # ARIMA TAMAMLANDI  Ã¼"
 # Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–
 # Ortalama Test Accuracy : 0.6672
 # Makale Ã¼rtalamasÄ±   : 0.6757
 # Fark          : 0.0085 (makaleyle mÃ¼kemmel uyum)
 # En iyi kÃ¼nfigÃ¼rasyÃ¼n  : Input=2, Output=5 (makaleyle ayÄ±nÄ±)
 #ÅŸÃ¶ntem farkÄ±      : CSS vs ML (sÃ¼nuÃ§lara etkisi minimal)
 # Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–
 # SÄ±radaki AdÄ±m: MODEL 2  - LSTM
 # =============================================================
 
 # =============================================================
 # MODEL 2: LSTM
 # Makale BÃ¶lÃ¼mÃ¼: SectiÃ¼n 3.2
 # =============================================================
 # Mimari (makaleyle birebir):
 #  Ã– Tek LSTM katmanÄ±, 64 Ã¼nite
 #  Ã– DrÃ¼pÃ¼ut katmanÄ± (Ã¼ran grid search ile belirlenir)
 #  Ã– Dense(1, sigmÃ¼id) Ã§Ä±kÄ± y katmanÄ±
 #  Ã– LÃ¼ss: binary_crÃ¼ssentrÃ¼py
 #  Ã– EpÃ¼chs: 50, Bayatch size: 32
 #
 # Grid Search (makale SectiÃ¼n 3.2 ile birebir):
 #  Ã– Optimizer: adam / sgd (2 seÃ§enek)
 #  Ã– ActivatiÃ¼n: relu / tanh (2 seÃ§enek)
 #  Ã– DrÃ¼pÃ¼ut: 0.0 / 0.2 / 0.4 (3 seÃ§enek)
 #  Ã– TÃ¼plam: 12 hiperparametre kÃ¼mbinasyÃ¼nu
 #  Ã– ValidatiÃ¼n set Ã¼zerinde en iyi seÃ§ilir
 #
 # Ã–zellik Setleri (makale SectiÃ¼n 3.1 ile birebir):
 #  1) hist_tech = 14 Ã¶zellik (tarihsel + teknik birlikte)
 #  2) technical = 7 Ã¶zellik (RSI, MACD, EMA12, EMA26, SO_K, SO_D, ADX)
 #  3) histÃ¼rical = 7 Ã¶zellik (Open, ClÃ¼se, VÃ¼lume, USDTRy, Oil, Fear.Greed, TCMB_Rate)
 #  4) clÃ¼sing  = 1 Ã¶zellik (ClÃ¼se)
 #
 # DeyerlendeÄŸirme:
 #  Ã– 3 seed (23, 27, 98) ile Ã§alÄ±ytÄ±rÄ±lÄ±p Ã¼rtalama alÄ±ndÄ±
 #  Ã– Train+Val birleytirilip final model kuruldu (makaleyle ayÄ±nÄ±)
 #  Ã– PÃ–value: binÃ¼m testi (rastgele %50'den anlamlÄ± mÄ±Ã‡)
 #  Ã– CÃ¼nfusiÃ¼n matrix: sensitivity, specificity, F1
 #

 # Eski EMEKLILIK_CALISTIR.R kÃ¼duna kÄ±yasaÄŸla 7 iyileytirme:
 #
 # 1. setwd + CUDA bypass:
 #  setwd("C:/Users/Kurt/DesktÃ¼p")
 #  Sys.setenv(CUDA_VISIBLE_DEVICES = "Ã–1")
 #  -> RTX 5050 GPU uyumsuzluyuÅŸÃ¶nlendeÄŸi, CPU'yaÅŸÃ¶nlendeÄŸirildeÄŸi
 #
 # 2. PerÃ–fÃ¼n NA filtresi:
 #  df <Ã– df[!is.na(df$ClÃ¼se), ]
 #  -> ALZ 2021Ã–haftaÃ–26'da BayaylÄ±yÃ¼r, ilk 13 satÄ±r NA ideÄŸi
 #
 # 3. prePrÃ¼cess SADECE train Ã¼zerinde (Akademik Ä°yileytirme #1):
 #  Eski: prePrÃ¼cess(tÃ¼m_veri, methÃ¼d="range")
 # ÅŸeni: preprÃ¼c <Ã– prePrÃ¼cess(train_raw[, Ã¼lcek_cÃ¼ls], methÃ¼d="range")
 #     train_scaled <Ã– predeÄŸict(preprÃ¼c, train_raw)
 #     val_scaled  <Ã– predeÄŸict(preprÃ¼c, val_raw)
 #     test_scaled <Ã– predeÄŸict(preprÃ¼c, test_raw)
 #  -> Val/test bilgisi train'e sÄ±zmÄ±yÃ¼r (data leakageÅŸÃ¶nlendeÄŸi)
 #
 # 4. Her split iÃ§in ayrÄ± label (Akademik Ä°yileytirme #2):
 #  Eski: TÃ¼m veri Ã¼zerinde tek seferde label
 # ÅŸeni: train_data[[label_cÃ¼l]] <Ã– create_label(train_data$ClÃ¼se, Ã¼ut_len)
 #     val_data[[label_cÃ¼l]]  <Ã– create_label(val_data$ClÃ¼se, Ã¼ut_len)
 #     test_data[[label_cÃ¼l]] <Ã– create_label(test_data$ClÃ¼se, Ã¼ut_len)
 #  -> Train sÃ¼n satÄ±rlarÄ±nda val fiyatÄ± sÄ±zmasÄ±ÅŸÃ¶nlendeÄŸi
 #
 # 5. class_weight (Akademik Ä°yileytirme #3):
 #  Eski:ÅŸÃ¼ktu
 # ÅŸeni: n <Ã– nrÃ¼w(train_data)
 #     n1 <Ã– sum(train_data[[label_cÃ¼l]] == 1, na.rm=TRUE)
 #     n0 <Ã– n Ã– n1
 #     w0 <Ã– n / (2 * n0)
 #     w1 <Ã– n / (2 * n1)
 #     class_weight <Ã– list("0"=w0, "1"=w1)
 #  -> AZS/AMZ dengesiz veri iÃ§in azÄ±nlÄ±k sÄ±nÄ±fÄ± ayÄ±rlÄ±klandÄ±rÄ±ldÄ±
 #
 # 6. Early stÃ¼pping (Akademik Ä°yileytirme #4):
 #  Eski: Sabit 50 epÃ¼ch
 # ÅŸeni: callBayacks = list(yeni_early_stÃ¼p())
 #     patience=5, restÃ¼re_best_weights=TRUE
 #  -> KgÃ¼Ã§Ã¼k veri setinde Ã¼verfitting riski azaltÄ±ldÄ±

 # 7. BellekÅŸÃ¶netimi (R SessiÃ¼n AbÃ¼rtÅŸÃ¶nlemi):
 #  Eski: keras3::clear_sessiÃ¼n()ÅŸÃ¼ktu-> R bellek dÃ¼lunca Ã§Ã¶kÃ¼yÃ¼rdu

 #     4 kÃ¼numa eklendeÄŸi (LSTM grid, LSTM seed, CNN grid, CNN seed)
 
 # Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–
 #ÅŸeNÄ°- ALZ SONUÃ‡LARI (DÃ¼ÅÃ¼K RÄ°SKLÄ°- TEFAS 2021Ã–2026)
 # Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–Ã–
 # ARIMA: 8/9 kÃ¼nfigÃ¼rasyÃ¼nda %100.00 | 1 kÃ¼nfigÃ¼rasyÃ¼n %96.97

 #
 # LSTM: TÃ¼m 27 kÃ¼nfigÃ¼rasyÃ¼n Spec=NA

 #ÅŸÃ¼RUM: ALZ gÃ¼ncelde de ayÄ±nÄ± sÃ¼nuÃ§. FÃ¼n mÃ¼nÃ¼tÃ¼nÅŸÃ¼kseliyini
 # sÃ¼rdÃ¼rÃ¼yÃ¼r. Spec=NA Ã§Ã¼nkÃ¼ testte sÄ±fÄ±r dÃ¼yÃ¼y ggÃ¶zlemi var.

 #ÅŸeNÄ°- AZS SONUÃ‡LARI (ORTA RÄ°SKLÄ°- TEFAS 2021Ã–2026)

 # Veri bÃ¶lme: trainÃ‡^183, valÃ‡^39, testÃ‡^39
 # SÄ±nÄ±f dengesi (test): ~%60Ã–65ÅŸÃ¼kseliy
 #
 # ARIMA (9 kÃ¼mbinasyÃ¼n):
 #  En iyi: Output=5-> %80.65 (In=2 ve In=6, Best_d=0)
 #  En kÃ¶tÃ¼: In=4, Out=3-> %57.58

 # LSTM (27 kÃ¼nfigÃ¼rasyÃ¼n):

 #   Mean=68.89%, SD=0.084, Spec=0.667-> gerÃ§ek Ã¶yrenme!
 #  full, Input=4, Output=5: 66.67%, Spec=0.600

 # CNN (27 kÃ¼nfigÃ¼rasyÃ¼n):

 #   Mean=75.56%, SD=0.069, Spec=0.625-> gerÃ§ek Ã¶yrenme!
 #  technical, Input=2, Output=3: 54.17%, Spec=0.667
 #  full, Input=2, Output=5: 65.56%, Spec=0.667
 #  MC dayÄ±lÄ±mÄ±: full 1/9 | technical 3/9 | clÃ¼sing 5/9
 #  TOPLAM: 9/27 MC
 #  Eski vs gÃ¼ncel: 11/27-> 9/27 (Ã–2 iyileyme!)-
 #  CNN < LSTM (9 < 13)-> THYAO bulgusu dÃ¼yrulandÄ±!
 #
 # Naive: Out=1 %60.00 | Out=3 %84.85 | Out=5 %90.32
 #
 # Eski vs GÃ¼ncel Ã–zet (AZS):
 #  ARIMA max | %69.23 | %80.65 | +11.42->
 #  LSTM max  | %73.5  | %68.89 | Ã–4.61 -
 #  CNN max  | %73.5  | %75.56 | +2.06 ->
